 " Finance Minister Jaitley said that the country's shopkeepers, traders and retailers will feel that doing official business in a formal manner is a better way than a parallel economy in an informal way
 unhone kaha ki pichley kai dashakon main bhartiya itihaas main is tarah ke bade faisle kii barabari kaa koi doosraa faisla nahin dikhaai detaa he jo ki naitik rup se itnaa sahi ho jisamen har eemaandaar vyakti ne yah mana he ki use chintit hone kii koi jarurat nahin he
 Jaitley admitted that the high denomination notes have been invalidated, but later some more legal steps will need to be taken to eliminate it altogether
 unhone kaha, "yah samajhnaa mahatvapurn hoga ki pichley 70 saalon se desh main yah saamaanya baat thi
 a parallel economy was going on in India, it was common practice to have formal as well as informal economy, it had become a part of our life
 " Large amounts of currency were in circulation outside the banking system
 desh kaa kar aadhaar kaaphi simit bana hua he
 The banking system had become challenging, if not fragile
 "meraa maananaa he ki jis maahaul main ham kaam kar rahe the vah saamaanya nahin tha
 This one decision has now defined a new normal for India
 " vittamantri ne is sambandh main udhaaharan dete hue kaha ki jis prakaar doorsanchaar kranti jise bharat main shur nahin kiya gaya balki yah ho gaya, usee prakaar aane vaale 5 se 8 saal main nayaa saamaanya kuch alag hi hoga
 “we will be in a completely different kind of economy
 " Talking about the major challenges facing the Indian economy, Arun Jaitley said that the ability to support the bank's growth was limited due to npas and their lending capabilities being questionable
 unhone yah bhi kaha ki nijee kshetra nivesh nahin laa rahaa or vaishvik narmi ke kaaran samasya badhati ja rahi he
 The Finance Minister said, "now let's see the effect of this decision in the medium and long term
 isse achaanak bainkon kii sasti dar par karj dene kii kshamta bad gayi he
 The ability of the Indian bank system to support growth, economy and economic growth had become highly questionable
 "tippaniyan He said that banks have suddenly come in abundant funds
 "ab is saste kosh ko companiyon, vyapaar, krishi, buniyadi dhaanche ko sasti dar par diya ja rahaa he
 "jaitley said," In the long run, it will change the way traders do business, how we manage the domestic budget
 yah bainkon main len-dein ko badhayega, hamaare paas saaf-suthri or badi arthvyavastha, badi karadhaan pranali hogi
 "(this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) notebandi kii ghoshnaa ke das din baad vitt mantri ne shuukravaar ko kaha ki sarkaar ke is kadam se bainkon ko vyavsaayiyon, vyapaariyon, krishi or dhanchaagat pariyojnaon ke liye sasti daron par karj dene main madad milegi jabaki iske saath hi nakli noton kii samanaantar vyavastha par ankush lagane kaa bhi kaam hoga
 Jaitley said at an event here, "as far as its implementation is concerned, i don't think it could have been done better than it has been done right now
" " unhone kaha ki bina kisi saamaajik samasya or aarthik gadabadi ke itani badi maatra main mudra ko arthtantr se nikaalnaa ek badi uplabdhi he
 He said, "whenever the currency is changed, there is initial inconvenience, but no such major incident happened in the country and it is slowly progressing smoothly with each passing day
 bainkon ke saamne line choti hoti ja rahi hai
 "jaitley said," In the next one to two weeks we have to make sure that the currency reaches the rural areas of the country where it is much needed
 haal ke samay main yah duniya main sambhavat: sabase bada mudra badlaav hua he
 " vittamantri jetali ne kaha ki desh ke dukandaaron, vyapaariyon or khudara vikritaon ko yah mahasoos hoga ki aupchaarik dhang se aadhikarik kaarobaar karnaa anaupchaarik tareeke kii samanaantar arthvyavastha ke mukaable kahin behatar tarika he
 He said that in the last several decades, there is no other judgment in Indian history to equal such a big decision which is so morally correct in which every honest person has believed that there is no need to be worried
 
 jetali ne sweekaar kiya ki unche mulya varg ke noton ko amaanya kar diya gaya he, lekin baad main ise puri tarah samaapt karne ke liye kuch or kanoonee kadam uthaane kii jarurat hogi
 He said, "it will be important to understand that this was common in the country for the last 70 years
 bharat main ek samanaantar arthvyavastha chal rahi thi, aupchaarik ke saath saath anaupchaarik arthvyavastha kaa bhi chalan saamaanya baat thi, yah hamaare jivan kaa hissaa ban gaya tha
 " baking pranali se baahar badi maatra main mudra prachlan main thi
 The tax base of the country remains quite limited
 banking pranali najuk nahin to chunauteepurn ban gai thi
 “I believe the environment in which we were working was not normal
 is ek faisle ne ab bharat ke liye nayaa saamaanya paribhaashit kiya he
 "the Finance Minister gave an example in this regard, saying that just like the telecom revolution which was not started in India but it happened, the new normal will be different in the coming 5 to 8 years
 "ham puri tarah se alag tarah kii arthvyavastha main honge
 " bhartiya arthvyavastha ke samaksh badi chunautiyon ke bare main arun jetali ne kaha ki enpie tathaa unki karj dene kii kshamta sandigdh hone se bank kii vruddhi ko samarthan dene kii kaabiliyat simitthi
 He also said that private sector is not bringing investment and the problem is increasing due to global softening
 vittamantri ne kaha, "ab madhyam evam dirghakaal main is nirnay ke prabhaav ko dekhte hai
 This has suddenly increased the ability of banks to lend at cheaper rates
 vruddhi, arthvyavastha tathaa aarthik vruddhi ko samarthan dene kii bhartiya bank pranali kii kshamta atyant sandigdh ho gai thi
 "comments unhone kaha ki bainkon ke paas achaanak se sasta kosh prachur maatra main aa gaya he

 6 disambar se pehle iskaa nirnay aana chahie agar isse pehle nirnay nahin aata to ham pradhanmantri modi se aagrah karenge ki teen talaak kii tarah adhyadesh laaen or ayodhya main ram mandir banaaen

 intjaar kiijie usase pehle ram mandir kaa nirmaan prarambh ho jayega

 main agar magar main vishwaas nahin karata hum
 i am of the view that the construction of Ram's temple in Ayodhya will start in 2019

 supreme court isamen apane str par nirnay karegaa

 roak lagani chahie vah khatm hona chahie

 sabhi ko court kaa hi faisla sweekaar hoga

 kasee tyaagi bole ki ram mandir par hamaari party kii raay saaf he ki ye yaa court ke faisle bane yaa phir aam sahmati se, lekin aam sahmati ban nahin pai hai isliye sabko court ke faisle kaa intjaar karnaa chahie chaahe kisi ke paksh main aaye
